The goal of this project is to design and develop a portfolio website for Maisonadrian, an established copywriting brand. The website should serve as a dynamic representation of the user’s professional identity, emphasizing the transformative power of words, brand storytelling, and the philosophical approach behind the craft of copywriting. The site must combine an intellectual aura with a minimalist design, reflecting the user’s unique approach to the art of writing.

Key Considerations:
Philosophical undertones: Each section should not merely state facts but express a deeper reflection on the role of words in the shaping of brands and cultures.

Minimalist aesthetic: The website should be clean, modern, and functional, with space for the written word to breathe, without unnecessary visual clutter.

Professional yet approachable: The tone should reflect both professionalism and intellectual depth, making the user’s work feel both authoritative and inspiring.

1. About Me Section
Purpose: This section introduces the user, Maisonadrian, while conveying a sense of intellectual gravitas, rooted in a philosophical outlook on writing and communication.

Brand Name: The website will be built under the brand name Maisonadrian. It is important that the full real name ("Adrian Münch") is not disclosed.

Core Services: Highlight the user’s primary offerings in copywriting, including:

Social Media Captions

Newsletters

Story Editing

SEO Titles

Philosophical Context: The user’s services should be presented within a larger, intellectual context. The text should evoke the idea that words are not simply tools of communication but a bridge between human understanding and emotional connection. Convey how writing shapes culture, brand identity, and social movements.

Example Philosophical Text for About Me Section:

"In a world where attention spans grow ever shorter, the power of the written word lies not in its length but in its impact. Maisonadrian does not simply write; Maisonadrian crafts messages that resonate deeply with the reader, transforming mere thoughts into powerful catalysts for action. Writing is an art—one that shapes how we perceive the world, how we communicate with one another, and how we define our brands. Words are the silent architects of thought and perception. In this craft, I find my purpose."

2. Services Section
Purpose: This section outlines the specific copywriting services provided by Maisonadrian. It must go beyond listing services and instead present them as integral tools to create impactful and lasting change for clients.

Primary Service Offerings:

Social Media Captions: Crafting concise, compelling, and brand-consistent captions that drive engagement and form connections.

Newsletters: Writing thought-provoking and action-driven newsletters that engage readers emotionally and intellectually.

Story Editing: Editing and curating social media stories, refining them for clarity, tone, and emotional impact.

SEO Title Writing: Creating SEO-optimized titles that not only rank well but also engage and captivate human readers.

Philosophical Approach: Each service should be framed with a reflection on the transformative power of language. The tone should suggest that writing is an essential tool of influence, helping brands connect deeply with their audience in meaningful ways.

Example Philosophical Text for Services Section:

"Writing is not just about putting words on paper; it is about creating meaning, context, and connection. At Maisonadrian, we understand that the right words can bridge the gap between a brand’s vision and its audience’s needs. Each caption, each newsletter, and each SEO title is crafted with the precision of a sculptor shaping marble—stripped of all excess and focused entirely on the emotional and intellectual impact it will leave behind."

3. Portfolio Section
Purpose: This section will showcase the user’s copywriting projects, demonstrating expertise and the intellectual approach to writing that Maisonadrian stands for.

Portfolio Content: Initially, the portfolio should include conceptual or placeholder projects. These can consist of:

Modified social media captions

Example newsletter sections

SEO titles for various industries

Edited stories for social media

These examples will be replaced as actual client work is acquired.

Instagram Integration: Since the user has an Instagram account for showcasing work, include a link to the Instagram profile: Maison_Adrian. The Instagram page will also serve as a living portfolio and an extension of the website’s presence.

4. Contact Section
Purpose: The contact page must encourage potential clients to reach out in an inviting, professional, and subtle manner, ensuring that the user’s services are easily accessible.

Contact Information: Include the following contact details:

Email: Maisonadrian@gmx.de

Instagram Link: Maison_Adrian Instagram

Call to Action: The tone should balance between being friendly and authoritative. Here is an example:

"Let’s create something meaningful. If you’re interested in collaborating or discussing how the power of words can elevate your brand, reach out today. I look forward to bringing your vision to life."

5. Legal Section
Purpose: The legal section is essential for ensuring compliance with regulations, even if placeholder content is used for now.

Impressum & Privacy Policy: Initially, placeholder text such as "Impressum and Privacy Policy coming soon" should be displayed.

6. Design and Aesthetic Requirements
Purpose: The website’s design must match the brand’s minimalist and philosophical values while ensuring the content is easily readable and engaging.

Color Scheme: The design should incorporate neutral tones—black, white, and grays—to create a timeless, clean aesthetic.

Typography: Use modern and clean fonts, such as Roboto for body text and Lora for headings, to provide clarity and legibility.

Logo: If available, the user’s logo should be displayed prominently on the homepage.

7. Future Expansion and SEO Considerations
Purpose: While the initial website design will be simple, it should be developed with future growth in mind. SEO optimization should be integrated from the start.

SEO Strategy: Ensure that the website’s structure supports SEO best practices, including:

Clean URL structures

Proper heading hierarchy (H1, H2, H3)

Alt text for images

Optimized meta descriptions and title tags for each page

Domain and Hosting: The user plans to acquire a custom domain (e.g., maisonadrian.com) in the future. The developer should ensure that the website is easily transferable to a custom domain when ready.

Conclusion
The Maisonadrian portfolio website should be a combination of intellectual depth and professional presentation. It should not just be a space to showcase copywriting services, but a philosophical statement on how words, when crafted with care, can transform brands and shape cultures.

```jsx
// src/App.jsx
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route } from 'react-router-dom';
import Header from './components/Header';
import Footer from './components/Footer';
import About from './pages/About';
import Services from './pages/Services';
import Portfolio from './pages/Portfolio';
import Contact from './pages/Contact';
import Legal from './pages/Legal';

function App() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <div className="min-h-screen flex flex-col bg-white text-gray-900">
        <Header />
        <main className="flex-grow container mx-auto px-4 py-8">
          <Routes>
            <Route path="/" element={<About />} />
            <Route path="/services" element={<Services />} />
            <Route path="/portfolio" element={<Portfolio />} />
            <Route path="/contact" element={<Contact />} />
            <Route path="/legal" element={<Legal />} />
          </Routes>
        </main>
        <Footer />
      </div>
    </Router>
  );
}

export default App;
```

```jsx
import React from 'react';

function Services() {
  const services = [
    {
      title: "Social Media Captions",
      description: "Crafting concise, compelling, and brand-consistent captions that drive engagement and form connections."
    },
    {
      title: "Newsletters",
      description: "Writing thought-provoking and action-driven newsletters that engage readers emotionally and intellectually."
    },
    {
      title: "Story Editing",
      description: "Editing and curating social media stories, refining them for clarity, tone, and emotional impact."
    },
    {
      title: "SEO Title Writing",
      description: "Creating SEO-optimized titles that not only rank well but also engage and captivate human readers."
    }
  ];

  return (
    <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto">
      <h1 className="font-lora text-4xl mb-8 font-semibold">Services</h1>
      <p className="text-lg mb-12 font-roboto leading-relaxed">
        Writing is not just about putting words on paper; it is about creating meaning, context, and connection. At Maisonadrian, we understand that the right words can bridge the gap between a brand's vision and its audience's needs. Each caption, each newsletter, and each SEO title is crafted with the precision of a sculptor shaping marble—stripped of all excess and focused entirely on the emotional and intellectual impact it will leave behind.
      </p>
      <div className="grid gap-8">
        {services.map((service, index) => (
          <div key={index} className="border-l-2 border-gray-800 pl-6 py-2">
            <h2 className="font-lora text-2xl mb-2">{service.title}</h2>
            <p className="font-roboto text-gray-700">{service.description}</p>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export default Services;
```

```jsx
// src/components/Header.jsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Link, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';

function Header() {
  const [isMenuOpen, setIsMenuOpen] = useState(false);
  const location = useLocation();

  const links = [
    { path: '/', text: 'About' },
    { path: '/services', text: 'Services' },
    { path: '/portfolio', text: 'Portfolio' },
    { path: '/contact', text: 'Contact' },
  ];

  const isActive = (path) => location.pathname === path;

  return (
    <header className="bg-white border-b border-gray-100">
      <nav className="container mx-auto px-4 py-6">
        <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
          <Link to="/" className="font-lora text-2xl font-semibold">
            Maisonadrian
          </Link>

          {/* Mobile menu button */}
          <button
            className="md:hidden"
            onClick={() => setIsMenuOpen(!isMenuOpen)}
          >
            <svg className="w-6 h-6" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
              <path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" strokeWidth="2" d="M4 6h16M4 12h16M4 18h16" />
            </svg>
          </button>

          {/* Desktop menu */}
          <div className="hidden md:flex space-x-8">
            {links.map((link) => (
              <Link
                key={link.path}
                to={link.path}
                className={`font-roboto ${
                  isActive(link.path)
                    ? 'text-gray-900 font-medium'
                    : 'text-gray-600 hover:text-gray-900'
                }`}
              >
                {link.text}
              </Link>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Mobile menu */}
        {isMenuOpen && (
          <div className="md:hidden mt-4 space-y-4">
            {links.map((link) => (
              <Link
                key={link.path}
                to={link.path}
                className={`block font-roboto ${
                  isActive(link.path)
                    ? 'text-gray-900 font-medium'
                    : 'text-gray-600 hover:text-gray-900'
                }`}
                onClick={() => setIsMenuOpen(false)}
              >
                {link.text}
              </Link>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </nav>
    </header>
  );
}

export default Header;
```

# Project Summary
The Maisonadrian Portfolio Website is designed to showcase the work of Maisonadrian, an established copywriting brand. The website serves as a dynamic representation of the user's professional identity, emphasizing the transformative power of words and brand storytelling through a minimalist design. It aims to provide an intellectual yet approachable tone, reflecting the unique philosophy behind the craft of copywriting.

# Project Module Description
The website includes the following functional modules:
1. **About Me Section**: Introduces Maisonadrian with a focus on the philosophical approach to writing.
2. **Services Section**: Details the copywriting services offered, framed within a broader intellectual context.
3. **Portfolio Section**: Displays copywriting projects, initially using placeholder content.
4. **Contact Section**: Provides contact information and encourages potential clients to reach out.
5. **Legal Section**: Contains necessary legal disclaimers and policies.

# Directory Tree
```
react_template/
├── README.md                  # Project documentation
├── eslint.config.js           # ESLint configuration
├── index.html                 # Main HTML file
├── package.json               # Project metadata and dependencies
├── postcss.config.js          # PostCSS configuration
├── public/data/example.json    # Example data file
├── src/
│   ├── App.jsx                # Main application component
│   ├── components/
│   │   ├── Footer.jsx         # Footer component
│   │   └── Header.jsx         # Navigation header component
│   ├── index.css              # Global styles
│   ├── main.jsx               # Entry point for React application
│   └── pages/
│       ├── About.jsx          # About section component
│       ├── Contact.jsx        # Contact section component
│       ├── Legal.jsx          # Legal section component
│       ├── Portfolio.jsx       # Portfolio section component
│       └── Services.jsx       # Services section component
├── tailwind.config.js         # Tailwind CSS configuration
└── vite.config.js             # Vite configuration
```

# File Description Inventory
- **README.md**: Contains project overview and setup instructions.
- **eslint.config.js**: Configuration for ESLint to maintain code quality.
- **index.html**: The main HTML structure of the web application.
- **package.json**: Lists project dependencies and scripts.
- **postcss.config.js**: Configuration for PostCSS processing.
- **example.json**: Contains example data for testing.
- **src/App.jsx**: Main component that sets up routing and layout.
- **src/components/**: Contains reusable components like Header and Footer.
- **src/pages/**: Contains page components for each section of the website.
- **tailwind.config.js**: Configuration file for Tailwind CSS.
- **vite.config.js**: Configuration for Vite as the build tool.

# Technology Stack
- **React**: JavaScript library for building user interfaces.
- **JavaScript**: Programming language used for client-side scripting.
- **Tailwind CSS**: Utility-first CSS framework for styling.
- **Vite**: Build tool that provides a fast development environment.
- **React Router**: Library for routing in React applications.

# Usage
To set up and run the project:
1. Install dependencies:
   ```bash
   pnpm install
   ```
2. Run the development server:
   ```bash
   pnpm run dev
   ```

# Project Summary
The Maison Adrian Portfolio Website serves as a professional showcase for Maison Adrian, a strategic copywriting brand. This dynamic platform highlights the art of persuasive writing and brand storytelling through a modern, minimalist design. The website aims to connect direct-to-consumer (DTC) brands with impactful copy that drives engagement and conversions, reflecting the unique philosophy of the brand.

# Project Module Description
The website includes the following functional modules:
1. **About Me Section**: Introduces Maison Adrian with an expanded bio focused on the strategic approach to copywriting.
2. **Services Section**: Clearly outlines the copywriting services offered, emphasizing their role in brand communication.
3. **Portfolio Section**: Displays selected work with detailed project descriptions, showcasing the effectiveness of the copywriting services.
4. **Contact Section**: Provides contact information and a form for potential clients to reach out.
5. **Testimonials Section**: Features client feedback to enhance credibility and showcase success stories.
6. **Legal Section**: Contains necessary legal disclaimers and policies.

# Directory Tree
```
react_template/
├── README.md                  # Project documentation
├── eslint.config.js           # ESLint configuration
├── index.html                 # Main HTML file
├── package.json               # Project metadata and dependencies
├── postcss.config.js          # PostCSS configuration
├── public/data/example.json    # Example data file
├── src/
│   ├── App.jsx                # Main application component
│   ├── components/
│   │   ├── Footer.jsx         # Footer component with branding and links
│   │   └── Header.jsx         # Navigation header component with CTA buttons
│   ├── index.css              # Global styles
│   ├── main.jsx               # Entry point for React application
│   └── pages/
│       ├── About.jsx          # About section component with expanded bio
│       ├── Contact.jsx        # Contact section component with email and form
│       ├── Legal.jsx          # Legal section component
│       ├── Portfolio.jsx      # Portfolio section component with project descriptions
│       └── Services.jsx       # Services section component detailing offerings
├── tailwind.config.js         # Tailwind CSS configuration
└── vite.config.js             # Vite configuration
```

# File Description Inventory
- **README.md**: Contains project overview and setup instructions.
- **eslint.config.js**: Configuration for ESLint to maintain code quality.
- **index.html**: The main HTML structure of the web application.
- **package.json**: Lists project dependencies and scripts.
- **postcss.config.js**: Configuration for PostCSS processing.
- **example.json**: Contains example data for testing.
- **src/App.jsx**: Main component that sets up routing and layout.
- **src/components/**: Contains reusable components like Header and Footer.
- **src/pages/**: Contains page components for each section of the website.
- **tailwind.config.js**: Configuration file for Tailwind CSS.
- **vite.config.js**: Configuration for Vite as the build tool.

# Technology Stack
- **React**: JavaScript library for building user interfaces.
- **JavaScript**: Programming language used for client-side scripting.
- **Tailwind CSS**: Utility-first CSS framework for styling.
- **Vite**: Build tool that provides a fast development environment.
- **React Router**: Library for routing in React applications.

# Usage
To set up and run the project:
1. Install dependencies:
   ```bash
   pnpm install
   ```
2. Run the development server:
   ```bash
   pnpm run dev
   ```
